#shanxi_events.1 and shanxi_events.2 replaced by intro screen

country_event = { # The Railway Discussion
	id = shanxi_events.2
	title = shanxi_events.2.t
	desc = shanxi_events.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_tongpu_railway
	is_triggered_only = yes #triggered from league_collapse.2 #Should be Jan 5thish
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = shanxi_events.3 days = 10 }
			QIE = {
				country_event = { id = shanxi_qing_aid_events.1 days = 1 } #Train Talks Derailed in Taiyuan
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_events.2 option shanxi_events.2.a"
		name = shanxi_events.2.a
		add_political_power = -30
	}
}

country_event = { # Recap on the army situation.
	id = shanxi_events.3
	title = shanxi_events.3.t
	desc = shanxi_events.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_feng_and_yan_2
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_events.3 option shanxi_events.3.a"
		name = shanxi_events.3.a
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_events.3 option shanxi_events.3.b"
		name = shanxi_events.3.b #I want to know more about the army
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		country_event = shanxi_events.3001
	}
	after = {
		add_war_support = -0.025
		add_command_power = 30
	}
}

country_event = { # Black Monday Arrives
	id = shanxi_events.4
	title = shanxi_events.4.t
	desc = shanxi_events.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_taiyuan_panic
	is_triggered_only = yes #Scripted Effect fire_black_monday_events
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SHX_underdeveloped_mountain_economy
				add_idea = SHX_underdeveloped_mountain_economy1
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_events.4 option shanxi_events.4.a"
		name = shanxi_events.4.a
		add_stability = -0.10
	}
}

country_event = { # Yan Speaks to Beijing
	id = shanxi_events.5
	title = shanxi_events.5.t
	desc = shanxi_events.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHN_intelligence
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by league_collapse.57
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = Shanxi_open_for_investment
		hidden_effect = {
			QIE = {
				country_event = { id = shanxi_qing_aid_events.2 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_events.5 option shanxi_events.5.a"
		name = shanxi_events.5.a
		SHX_QIE_investment_medium = yes
		add_political_power = -20
		SHX_set_up_QIE_influence_game = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = shanxi_events.6 days = 2 }
		}
	}
}

		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_events.6 option shanxi_events.6.a"
		name = shanxi_events.6.a
		add_stability = -0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
			remove_from_coalition = yes
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_GMJ_leaves_coalition_tooltip
	}
}

country_event = { #Another Hard Year...
	id = shanxi_events.9
	title = shanxi_events.9.t
	desc = shanxi_events.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_shaanxi_poor
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by event shanxi_events.1, should go off Around September

	trigger = {
		has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
	}

	#This event helps even the odds by cutting down Yan's starting 20% Influence to either +10% or giving Feng an advantage of +5%.
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_events.9 option shanxi_events.9.a"
		name = shanxi_events.9.a #The Guominjun harnesses peasant discontentment
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_PATAUT }
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		SHX_strengthen_feng_large = yes
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_events.9 option shanxi_events.9.b"
		name = shanxi_events.9.b #The Provincial Government hurries to the rescue
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_AUTDEM }
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		add_political_power = -40
		SHX_strengthen_feng_medium = yes
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_events.9 option shanxi_events.9.c"
		name = shanxi_events.9.c #Loans from Beijing Alleviate Problems
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_political_power = 35
		SHX_QIE_investment_medium = yes
		SHX_strengthen_feng_small = yes
	}
}

country_event = { # Invite Foreign Advisors
	id = shanxi_military_events.1
	title = shanxi_military_events.1.t
	desc = shanxi_military_events.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by Focus SHX_invite_foreign_advisors
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_feng_advisors
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_military_events.1 option shanxi_military_events.1.a"
		name = shanxi_military_events.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_PATAUT }
			}
		}
		add_ideas = SHX_russian_aid
		SHX_strengthen_feng_medium = yes
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_military_events.1 option shanxi_military_events.1.b"
		name = shanxi_military_events.1.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_PATAUT }
			}
		}
		add_ideas = SHX_japanese_aid
		SHX_strengthen_feng_small = yes
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_military_events.1 option shanxi_military_events.1.c"
		name = shanxi_military_events.1.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 45
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_AUTDEM }
			}
		}
		add_ideas = SHX_german_aid
		SHX_strengthen_yan_medium = yes
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = shanxi_military_events.2 #Shanxi Commissars
	title = shanxi_military_events.2.t
	desc = shanxi_military_events.2.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_QIE_zhili_soldiers
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_military_events.2 option shanxi_military_events.2.a"
		name = shanxi_military_events.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_PATAUT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2 #Lock-in: After Oct-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1936.10.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_feng_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #Lock-in: After Jan-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1937.01.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_feng_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		trigger = { has_character = SHX_feng_yuxiang } #So if you already purged Yan, you have one option
		add_ideas = SHX_guominjun_commissars_idea
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		SHX_strengthen_feng_medium = yes
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_military_events.2 option shanxi_military_events.2.b"
		name = shanxi_military_events.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_AUTDEM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2 #Lock-in: After Oct-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1936.10.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_yan_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #Lock-in: After Jan-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1937.01.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_yan_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		trigger = { has_character = SHX_yan_xishan } #So if you already purged Feng, you have one option
		add_ideas = SHX_yan_commissars_idea
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		SHX_strengthen_yan_medium = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Go Yan or Go Feng for Policies
	id = shanxi_political_events.1
	title = shanxi_political_events.1.t
	desc = shanxi_political_events.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_shaanxi_poor
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = SHX_yan_feng_split
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_political_events.1 option shanxi_political_events.1.a"
		name = shanxi_political_events.1.a #Yan
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_AUTDEM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2 #Lock-in: After Oct-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1936.10.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_yan_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #Lock-in: After Jan-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1937.01.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_yan_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Lock-in: If Shanxi is already leaning towards one direction, it will pursue it
				SHX_feng_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SHX_Yan_purpose
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_political_events.1 option shanxi_political_events.1.b"
		name = shanxi_political_events.1.b #Feng
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_PATAUT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2 #Lock-in: After Oct-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1936.10.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_feng_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #Lock-in: After Jan-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1937.01.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_feng_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Lock-in: If Shanxi is already leaning towards one direction, it will pursue it
				SHX_yan_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SHX_Feng_purpose
		}
	}
}

			}
		}

		name = shanxi_political_events.5.a

			10 = {
				add_political_power = 25
			}
			40 = {
				add_political_power = 10
			}
			40 = {
				add_political_power = -10
			}
			10 = {
				add_political_power = -25
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #What a disgrace...

		name = shanxi_political_events.5.b

country_event = {
	id = shanxi_political_events.6  #Automobile Accidents Accidents in Taiyuan
	title = shanxi_political_events.6.t
	desc = shanxi_political_events.6.d
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by event shanxi_political_events.5
	picture = GFX_report_event_SIA_Car_Crash_Minister_Died

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj
			has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = shanxi_political_events.7 days = 7 } #The Governor and His People
		}
	}

	option = { #The incident is covered up
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_political_events.6 option shanxi_political_events.6.a"
		name = shanxi_political_events.6.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_AUTDEM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2 #Lock-in: After Oct-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1936.10.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_yan_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #Lock-in: After Jan-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1937.01.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_yan_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SHX_feng_sizhi = { is_political_advisor = no }
			}
			add_political_power = -40
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_feng_sizhi_helpful_tooltip
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -10
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_feng_sizhi_is_helpful_tooltip
		}
	}

	option = { #The scandal grows!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_political_events.6 option shanxi_political_events.6.b"
		name = shanxi_political_events.6.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_PATAUT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2 #Lock-in: After Oct-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1936.10.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_feng_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #Lock-in: After Jan-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1937.01.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_feng_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		SHX_strengthen_feng_small = yes
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = shanxi_agricultural_events.1 #Choosing Agricultural Path
	title = shanxi_agricultural_events.1.t
	desc = shanxi_agricultural_events.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_FNG_farmers
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = SHX_agricultural_reform_mission_timer
			country_event = { id = shanxi_agricultural_events.4 days = 7 } #A Tale of Two Generations
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_agricultural_events.1 option shanxi_agricultural_events.1.yan"
		name = shanxi_agricultural_events.1.yan
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_AUTDEM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5 #Lock-in: After Oct-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1936.10.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_yan_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #Lock-in: After Jan-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1937.01.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_yan_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Lock-in: After Mar-1937 SHX will stop choosing focuses related to the opposite side until the power struggle is won.
				date > 1937.03.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_feng_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SHX_yan_land_reform
			country_event = { id = shanxi_mission_tick_events.3 days = 5 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_Yan_Favored_10_Year_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { has_war = yes }
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SHX_agricultural_reform_mission_timer
				days = 400
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_reform_disrupted_by_war_tooltip
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_agricultural_events.1 option shanxi_agricultural_events.1.feng"
		name = shanxi_agricultural_events.1.feng
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_PATAUT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5 #Lock-in: After Oct-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1936.10.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_feng_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #Lock-in: After Oct-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1936.10.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_feng_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Lock-in: After mid 1937 SHX will stop choosing focuses related to the opposite side until the power struggle is won.
				date > 1937.06.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_yan_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SHX_feng_land_reform
			country_event = { id = shanxi_mission_tick_events.6 days = 5 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_Feng_Favored_10_Year_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = { has_war = yes }
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SHX_agricultural_reform_mission_timer
				days = 400
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_reform_disrupted_by_war_tooltip
		}
	}
}

	id = shanxi_agricultural_events.3
	title = shanxi_agricultural_events.3.t
	desc = shanxi_agricultural_events.3.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_farming

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_agricultural_events.3 option shanxi_agricultural_events.3.a"
		name = shanxi_agricultural_events.3.a #Slash wasteful projects!
		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				SHX_lian_tianxiang = { is_political_advisor = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_political_power > 60
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SHX_lian_tianxiang = { is_political_advisor = yes }
			}
			add_political_power = -50
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_lian_tianxiang_is_helpful_tooltip
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -100
			add_stability = -0.05
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_lian_tianxiang_helpful_tooltip
		}
	}
	option = { #Simp to QIE
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_agricultural_events.3 option shanxi_agricultural_events.3.b"
		name = shanxi_agricultural_events.3.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				SHX_wang_xiang = {
					OR = {
						is_political_advisor = yes
						is_second_in_command = yes
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_political_power < 25
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					AND = { #check if they have a non-QIE forpol rule set
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
						NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = SHX_FORPOL_QIE } }
					}
					has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_AUTDEM }
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = { SHX_QIE_influence_active = yes }
		if = {
			limit = {
				SHX_wang_xiang = {
					OR = {
						is_political_advisor = yes
						is_second_in_command = yes
					}
				}
			}
			add_political_power = 50
			SHX_QIE_investment_medium = yes #In this case Wang Xiang helped you get a better deal
			SHX_econ_update = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_Wang_Xiang_is_helpful_tooltip
		}
		else = {
			SHX_QIE_investment_medium = yes
			SHX_econ_update = yes
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_Wang_Xiang_helpful_tooltip
		}
	}
	option = { #Heavy taxes
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_agricultural_events.3 option shanxi_agricultural_events.3.c"
		name = shanxi_agricultural_events.3.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 33
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					SHX_su_tiren = { is_political_advisor = yes }
					SHX_su_tiren = { is_second_in_command = yes }
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_war_support > 0.50
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					SHX_su_tiren = { is_political_advisor = yes }
					SHX_su_tiren = { is_second_in_command = yes }
				}
			}
			add_war_support = -0.05
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_su_tiren_is_helpful_tooltip
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -50
			add_war_support = -0.1
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_su_tiren_helpful_tooltip
		}
	}
}

				}
			}
			random_owned_controlled_state = {

					NOT = {
						state = 1072
					}
				}

					type = industrial_complex
					damage = 0.25
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_xue_dubi_is_helpful_tooltip
		}

			SHX_strengthen_yan_medium = yes
		}
		else = {
			SHX_strengthen_feng_medium = yes
		}
	}
	option = {

		}

		}

	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_education_events.1 option shanxi_education_events.1.a"

		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_AUTDEM }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5 #Lock-in: After Oct-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1936.10.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_yan_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #Lock-in: After Jan-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1937.01.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_yan_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Lock-in: After Mar-1937 SHX will stop choosing focuses related to the opposite side until the power struggle is won.
				date > 1937.03.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_feng_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = shx_education_yan_path
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = shanxi_mission_tick_events.1 days = 5 }
		}

			base = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_path option = SHX_PATH_PATAUT }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5 #Lock-in: After Oct-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1936.10.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_feng_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3 #Lock-in: After Jan-1936 SHX should try to be more aggressive in choosing a side
				date > 1937.01.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup
				SHX_feng_is_winning_trigger = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #Lock-in: After Mar-1937 SHX will stop choosing focuses related to the opposite side until the power struggle is won.
				date > 1937.03.01
				has_active_mission = SHX_looming_gmj_coup

		country_event = shanxi_power_struggle_events.2
	}
	after = {

	}
}

		add_political_power = 25
		add_stability = 0.10
		clr_country_flag = SHX_yan_feng_split

		}

		}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {

			}
			set_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj

			}

				}

				focus = SHX_socialism

			}

				country_event = { id = shanxi_power_struggle_events.7 days = 10 }
				country_event = { id = shanxi_power_struggle_events.8 days = 15 }
			}
		}
		deactivate_advisor = SHX_feng_yuxiang_sic
	}
}
country_event = { # The Guominjun Revolution
	id = shanxi_power_struggle_events.4
	title = shanxi_power_struggle_events.4.t
	desc = shanxi_power_struggle_events.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_guominjun_soldiers
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Finally it is done
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_power_struggle_events.4 option shanxi_power_struggle_events.4.a"
		name = shanxi_power_struggle_events.4.a
		clr_country_flag = SHX_yan_feng_split
		add_political_power = 25
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_stability = 0.10
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.075
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.025
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			end_coalition = yes #Should clear the existing coalition Yan had
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = SHX_republican_united_front
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
				add_to_coalition = yes
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:radical_socialist }
				add_to_coalition = yes
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
				add_to_coalition = yes
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
				add_to_coalition = yes
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GMJ_republican_coalition_formed_tooltip
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj }
				clr_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj
			}
			set_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan

			add_power_balance_value = {
				id = SHX_power_balance
				value = 2.0
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = SHX_Yan_purpose
				}
				clr_country_flag = SHX_Yan_purpose
			}
			set_country_flag = SHX_Feng_purpose
			uncomplete_national_focus = {
				focus = SHX_doctrine_of_mean
				uncomplete_children = yes
			}
			set_country_leader_description = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				desc = SHX_feng_yuxiang_victory_leader_desc
			}
			SHX = {
				country_event = { id = shanxi_power_struggle_events.5 days = 5 }
				country_event = { id = shanxi_power_struggle_events.7 days = 10 }
				country_event = { id = shanxi_power_struggle_events.8 days = 15 }
			}
		}
		deactivate_advisor = SHX_feng_yuxiang_sic
		if = {

					create_wargoal = {
						target = SHX
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = shanxi_manchu_coup_events.2 #The Siege of Xi'an (the Invasion Begins)
	title = shanxi_manchu_coup_events.2.t
	desc = shanxi_manchu_coup_events.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_feng_looking_in_telescope

	is_triggered_only = yes #Fires for both QIE and SHX after the death of Wu Peifu and Cao Kun

	major = yes
	show_major = {
		OR = {
			tag = QIE
			tag = SHX
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_manchu_coup_events.2 option shanxi_manchu_coup_events.2.a"
		name = shanxi_manchu_coup_events.2.a #This is our chance
		trigger = { tag = SHX }
		transfer_state = 799 #Guanzhong (Xi'an)
		add_state_core = 799 #Guanzhong (Xi'an)
		799 = { set_demilitarized_zone = no } #Xi'an
		custom_override_tooltip = {
			tooltip = {
				localization_key = tooltip_create_division_template
				NAME = "Guomindang Minbing"
				LINE_1 = { localization_key = line_battalion_tt NAME = militia ICON = GFX_unit_militia_icon_small COUNT = 6 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_template = "Guomindang Minbing" }
				delete_unit_template_and_units = { division_template = "Guomindang Minbing" disband = yes } #no cheating
			}
			division_template = {
				name = "Guomindang Minbing" #KMT Militia
				division_names_group = CHYN_MIL_01
				regiments = {
					militia = { x = 0 y = 0 }
					militia = { x = 0 y = 1 }
					militia = { x = 0 y = 2 }
					militia = { x = 1 y = 0 }
					militia = { x = 1 y = 1 }
					militia = { x = 1 y = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		799 = {
			teleport_armies = {
				limit = { tag = QIE }
				to_state = 607 #Every QIE division in Xi'an goes to Luoyang
			}
			custom_override_tooltip = {
				tooltip = {
					localization_key = tooltip_spawn_units
					COUNT = 2
					TYPE = "Guomindang Minbing"
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Xi'an County Farmers' Militia\" division_template = \"Guomindang Minbing\" start_experience_factor = 0.60"
					owner = SHX
				}
				create_unit = {
					division = "name = \"Shaanxi Garrison Defectors\" division_template = \"Guomindang Minbing\" start_experience_factor = 0.60"
					owner = SHX
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_state = {
				teleport_armies = {
					limit = { tag = QIE }
					to_state = 615 #Every other QIE division in SHX territory goes to East Shanxi
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_manchu_coup_events.2 option shanxi_manchu_coup_events.2.b"
		name = shanxi_manchu_coup_events.2.b #We held up our end, they better do the same
		trigger = { tag = QIE }
	}
}

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = SHX }
				clr_country_flag = SHX_yan_feng_split
				set_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan
				set_country_flag = SHX_feng_manchu_coup_outcome_flag
				log = "KR_Event_Logging;SHX Game Progression - Feng Yuxiang, Manchu Coup, Survived Independent"
				clr_country_flag = SHX_Yan_purpose
				set_country_flag = SHX_Feng_purpose
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					popularity = -0.20
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_conservative
					popularity = 0.04
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = social_liberal
					popularity = 0.01
				}
				uncomplete_national_focus = {
					focus = SHX_doctrine_of_mean
					uncomplete_children = yes
				}
				complete_national_focus = SHX_a_higher_purpose
				complete_national_focus = SHX_socialism
				set_country_leader_description = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					desc = SHX_feng_yuxiang_victory_leader_desc
				}
				deactivate_advisor = SHX_feng_yuxiang_sic
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_completed_focus = SHX_republican_united_front
					}
					set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
					add_to_coalition = yes
					set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:radical_socialist }
					add_to_coalition = yes
					set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
					add_to_coalition = yes
					set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
					add_to_coalition = yes
					custom_effect_tooltip = GMJ_republican_coalition_formed_tooltip
				}
				add_war_support = 0.75 #Need to make up for -30% from strict neutrality and -20% from offensive war. Should add up to 25% War support which is enough for conscription.
				add_political_power = 200
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_manchu_coup_events.4 option shanxi_manchu_coup_events.4.a"
		name = shanxi_manchu_coup_events.4.a #Feng Yuxiang will complete the revolution!
		trigger = { tag = SHX }
		SHX_manchu_coup_setup_effect = yes
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_manchu_coup_events.4 option shanxi_manchu_coup_events.4.b"
		name = shanxi_manchu_coup_events.4.b #Yan Xishan will save China! (Tag Switch)
		trigger = {
			tag = SHX
			is_ai = no
		}
		SHX_manchu_coup_setup_effect = yes
		QIE = { change_tag_from = ROOT }
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_manchu_coup_events.4 option shanxi_manchu_coup_events.4.c"
		name = shanxi_manchu_coup_events.4.c #A New Imperial Commissioner Rises!
		trigger = { tag = QIE }
		effect_tooltip = { SHX_manchu_set_up_timer_effect = yes }
		custom_effect_tooltip = QIE_fear_fengtian
	}

		name = shanxi_manchu_coup_events.10.a

			add_stability = -0.25
			add_war_support = -0.25
		}

			add_stability = -0.10
			add_war_support = -0.10
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = SHX_central_plains_war_idea }
			remove_ideas = SHX_central_plains_war_idea
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = shanxi_japanese_infiltration_events.1 #Growing Japanese Infiltration
	title = shanxi_japanese_infiltration_events.1.t
	desc = {
		text = shanxi_japanese_infiltration_events.1.d.peace
		trigger = { NOT = { has_war_with = JAP } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = shanxi_japanese_infiltration_events.1.d.war
		trigger = { has_war_with = JAP }
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered event shanxi_advisor_events.13 #Komoto Daisaku's Appointment
	picture = GFX_report_event_JAP_kwantung

	trigger = {
		SHX_komoto_daisaku = { is_political_advisor = yes }
		NOT = { has_global_flag = JAP_defeated_by_china } #need to get infiltration before Sino-Japanese war ends
		JAP = {
			is_subject = no
			is_major = yes
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_japanese_infiltration_events.1 option shanxi_japanese_infiltration_events.1.a"
		name = shanxi_japanese_infiltration_events.1.a #An utter betrayal!
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = SHX_komoto_daisaku }
			retire_character = SHX_komoto_daisaku
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = SHX_su_tiren }
			retire_character = SHX_su_tiren
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = SHX_feng_sizhi }
			retire_character = SHX_feng_sizhi
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = SHX_han_fuju }
			retire_character = SHX_han_fuju
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = SHX_liu_yufen }
			retire_character = SHX_liu_yufen
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = SHX_tung_chi_mining_concern }
			remove_ideas = SHX_tung_chi_mining_concern
		}
		set_country_flag = SHX_tung_chi_mining_concern_abolished_flag
		if = {
			limit = {
				SHX_sun_chu = { is_political_advisor = no }
			}
			add_stability = -0.10
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_sun_chu_helpful_tooltip
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = -0.05
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_sun_chu_is_helpful_tooltip
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_japanese_infiltration_events.1 option shanxi_japanese_infiltration_events.1.b"
		name = shanxi_japanese_infiltration_events.1.b #Sweep it under the rug...
		if = {
			limit = {
				SHX_sun_chu = { is_political_advisor = no }
			}
			add_political_power = -200
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_sun_chu_helpful_tooltip
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -100
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_sun_chu_is_helpful_tooltip
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_japanese_allies_intel_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			JAP = {
				country_event = { id = shanxi_japanese_infiltration_events.2 days = 20 }
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = SHX_allowed_japanese_influence_flag
	}
}

				SHX_chih_kung_jen = { is_political_advisor = no }
			}

				mission = SHX_educational_reform_mission_timer
				days = -50
			}

		}
		else = {
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SHX_educational_reform_mission_timer
				days = -100
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_chih_kung_jen_is_helpful_tooltip
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				SHX_zhao_pilian = { is_political_advisor = no }
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = SHX_james_yens_literacy_campaign
				days = 365
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.02
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_zhao_pilian_helpful_tooltip
		}
		else = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = SHX_james_yens_literacy_campaign
				days = 400
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.035
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_zhao_pilian_is_helpful_tooltip
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist #A few student radicals slip in
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		SHX_QIE_investment_medium = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_qing_aid_events.9 option shanxi_qing_aid_events.9.b"
		name = shanxi_qing_aid_events.9.b #A bunch of pseudo-intellectual nonsense

		ai_chance = {
			base = 50

			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_political_power > 50
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 1.2
				has_political_power > 100
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				has_political_power < 50
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				has_political_power < 25
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				has_political_power < 0
			}

			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				SHX_zhao_daiwen = { is_political_advisor = yes }
			}
		}

				popularity = 0.02

country_event = {
	id = shanxi_advisor_events.1 #Hu Jingtong's appointment
	title = shanxi_advisor_events.1.t
	desc = shanxi_advisor_events.1.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_advisor_events.1 option shanxi_advisor_events.1.a"
		name = shanxi_advisor_events.1.a #We Look Forward to Working with You
		SHX_strengthen_feng_small = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = shanxi_advisor_events.40 #A Right Hand Man
	title = shanxi_advisor_events.40.t
	desc = {
		text = shanxi_advisor_events.40.d.1 #Yan's Men
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = shanxi_advisor_events.40.d.2 #Feng's Men
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered on Removal of a SIC

	trigger = { SHX = { NOT = { any_character = { is_second_in_command = yes } } } }

			SHX_zhao_daiwen = { has_advisor_role = second_in_command }

country_event = {
	id = shanxi_advisor_events.41 #A New Prime Minister
	title = shanxi_advisor_events.41.t
	desc = {
		text = shanxi_advisor_events.41.d.1 #Yan's Men
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = shanxi_advisor_events.41.d.2 #Feng's Men
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes #Trigged By EVENT: shanxi_endgame_events.12
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHI_nanjing_legislative_yuan_conference_hall

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_advisor_events.41 option shanxi_advisor_events.41.a"
		name = shanxi_advisor_events.41.a #Jia Jingde - Conservatives
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj
			SHX_jia_jingde = { has_advisor_role = second_in_command }
			#No need for special trigger since always no Zhao Daiwen.
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					SHX_zhao_daiwen = { is_second_in_command = yes }
					SHX_jia_jingde = { is_second_in_command = yes }
				}
			}
			add_political_power = 35
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -40
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = 0.05 }
		activate_advisor = SHX_jia_jingde_sic
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_advisor_events.41 option shanxi_advisor_events.41.b"
		name = shanxi_advisor_events.41.b #Wang Xiang - the German/Foreign Guy
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj
			SHX_wang_xiang = { has_advisor_role = second_in_command }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SHX_wang_xiang = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			add_political_power = 35
		}
		else = { add_political_power = -40 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.05 } #Stretch but maybe the DCP types sort of respect the German model. He also was involved with Rural and Education stuff, which is sort of the DCP platform anyway.
		activate_advisor = SHX_wang_xiang_sic
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_this_may_unlock_some_allies_in_the_future_tt
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_advisor_events.41 option shanxi_advisor_events.41.c"
		name = shanxi_advisor_events.41.c #Liang Huazhi - the Young Guard
		trigger = {
			SHX_liang_huazhi = { has_advisor_role = second_in_command }
			has_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SHX_liang_huazhi = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			add_political_power = 35
		}
		else = { add_political_power = -40 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = national_populist popularity = 0.05 }
		activate_advisor = SHX_liang_huazhi_sic
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_advisor_events.41 option shanxi_advisor_events.41.d"
		name = shanxi_advisor_events.41.d #Su Tiren - Pro Japan?
		trigger = {
			NOT = { SHX_komoto_daisaku = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			SHX_su_tiren = { has_advisor_role = second_in_command }
			has_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SHX_su_tiren = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			add_political_power = 35
		}
		else = { add_political_power = -40 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.05 }
		activate_advisor = SHX_su_tiren_sic
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_advisor_events.41 option shanxi_advisor_events.41.e"
		name = shanxi_advisor_events.41.e #Komoto Daisaku using Su Tiren as a puppet = Super Pro Japan
		trigger = {
			SHX_komoto_daisaku = { is_second_in_command = yes }
			has_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SHX_komoto_daisaku = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			add_political_power = 35
		}
		else = { add_political_power = -40 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.05 }
		activate_advisor = SHX_komoto_daisaku_sic
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_this_may_unlock_some_allies_in_the_future_tt
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_advisor_events.41 option shanxi_advisor_events.41.f"
		name = shanxi_advisor_events.41.f #Sun Yue - the Guominjun Stalwart
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan
			SHX_sun_yue = { has_advisor_role = second_in_command }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SHX_sun_yue = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			add_political_power = 35
		}
		else = { add_political_power = -40 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.05 }
		activate_advisor = SHX_sun_yue_sic
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_advisor_events.41 option shanxi_advisor_events.41.g"
		name = shanxi_advisor_events.41.g #Hu Jingyi - the Populist General
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan
			SHX_hu_jingyi = { has_advisor_role = second_in_command }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SHX_hu_jingyi = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			add_political_power = 35
		}
		else = { add_political_power = -40 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = 0.05 } #His brother leads the Shaanxi KMT.
		activate_advisor = SHX_hu_jingyi_sic
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_advisor_events.41 option shanxi_advisor_events.41.h"
		name = shanxi_advisor_events.41.h #Xue Dubi - the Civilian Counsel
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan
			SHX_xue_dubi = { has_advisor_role = second_in_command }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SHX_xue_dubi = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			add_political_power = 35
		}
		else = { add_political_power = -40 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.05 } #Similar agenda to the Soc Cons
		activate_advisor = SHX_xue_dubi_sic
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_advisor_events.41 option shanxi_advisor_events.41.i"
		name = shanxi_advisor_events.41.i #Yu Xinqing - the Red Priest
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan
			SHX_yu_xinqing = { has_advisor_role = second_in_command }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SHX_yu_xinqing = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			add_political_power = 35
		}
		else = { add_political_power = -40 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.05 } #CDL member otl
		activate_advisor = SHX_yu_xinqing_sic
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_advisor_events.41 option shanxi_advisor_events.41.j"
		name = shanxi_advisor_events.41.j #Shang Zhen - the KMT Stalwart
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan
			SHX_shang_zhen = { is_second_in_command = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SHX_shang_zhen = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			add_political_power = 35
		}
		else = { add_political_power = -40 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = 0.05 } #Okay kind of a stretch here, I guess non socialist KMT figures would end up classified as Pat Aut but all the other ideology slots get boosted. Besides, this guy was chil with PRC.
		activate_advisor = SHX_shang_zhen_sic
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.4 #Last Chance for Peace
	title = shanxi_zhifeng_events.4.t
	desc = {
		text = shanxi_zhifeng_events.4.d.1
		trigger = { QIE = { exists = yes } }
	}
	desc = {
		text = shanxi_zhifeng_events.4.d.2
		trigger = { QIE = { exists = no } }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_yan_car
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by focus SHX_out_of_beijing

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.4 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.4.a"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.4.a #I'd like to mull this over...
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			SHX_QIE_can_negotiate_check = yes
		}
		country_event = shanxi_zhifeng_events.5
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.4 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.4.b"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.4.b #We march to liberate China!
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				QIE = { has_war_with = FNG } #Zhifeng is active
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				QIE = {
					any_enemy_country = { owns_state = 613 } #An Enemy owns Nanjing
					has_war_with = FNG
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1000 #Don't want to set the other to 0 in case its the only option
				QIE = { has_completed_focus = QIE_purge_zhili }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01 #just in case this is the only option
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = SHX_FORPOL_QIE }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = SHX_FORPOL_QIE }
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			SHX_QIE_can_reject_negotiation_check = yes #Available if Beijing's influence is below 75% or if they have lost control of either the North or South
			NOT = { is_subject_of = QIE } #In case you get puppeted mid-event chain.
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			QIE = {
				country_event = { id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.6 days = 7 } #Taiyuan Takes a Hardline
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_zhifeng_no_negotiations_tooltip
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.4 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.4.c"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.4.c #Perhaps an accord can still be struck
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FNG = { exists = no } #Feng is dead
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 50 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 25 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				QIE = {
					NOT = {
						controls_state = 1048 #Wuhan
						controls_state = 608 #Beijing
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				QIE = { surrender_progress > 0.25 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.20
				QIE = {
					has_completed_focus = QIE_purge_zhili #SHX effectively unwilling to negotiate with Manchu QIE
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.01 #just in case this is the only option
				#check if they have a non-QIE forpol rule set
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = SHX_FORPOL_QIE } }
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_subject_of = QIE #If SHX got puppeted mid-chain, will force you to negotiate
				SHX_QIE_can_negotiate_check = yes #Available as long as Beijing owns both Xian and East Shanxi - if there's a scenario where they can own one but not both, deal with another day
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			QIE = {
				country_event = { id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.7 days = 1 } #Representatives Arrive from Taiyuan
			}
			SHX = {
				country_event = { id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.8 days = 3 } #Starting Point for Discussions
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_zhifeng_yes_negotiations_tooltip
		if = {
			limit = {
				SHX_QIE_can_reject_negotiation_check = no
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_zhifeng_forced_to_negotiate_tooltip
		}
	}
}

 ############################################
 ##- Maintenance Note from Chiang Kaishrek-##
 ############################################
 #The SHX-QIE Negotiation Event chain works across 4 files - Events, Scripted Effects, Scripted Loc, and Loc.
 #The Event File is fairly simple - each click will always lead to the next event in the chain (or to either acceptance/denial), adding and subtracting the "SHX_QIE_negotiation_value" each time along with War Support/QIE influence
 #There are 5 scripted that alter negotiations effects: add 1, add 2, add 3, minus 1, and minus 2.
 #Each is attached to a tooltip, which links to a the defined text to tell the player what selecting the option will press for.
 #Said defined text in the scripted loc will automatically calculate the predicted result and show it to the player.
 #There is one final scripted effect that concludes negotiations with an acceptance - thereby ending the event chain with whatever the current SHX_QIE_negotiation_value on the table
 #Because of the number of moving parts, I have decided to make the system somewhat brittle to ensure any issue is immediately visible.
 #The SHX_QIE_negotiation_value should ALWAYS be within 1-5.

country_event = {
	id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.8 #Taiyuan-Beijing Talks: Opening Round (SHX)
	title = shanxi_zhifeng_events.8.t
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_war_support > 0.64
		}
		text = shanxi_zhifeng_events.8.d.three
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_war_support > 0.59
		}
		text = shanxi_zhifeng_events.8.d.two
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_war_support < 0.60
		}
		text = shanxi_zhifeng_events.8.d.one
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_yan_speech
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by event option shanxi_zhifeng_events.4.c or shanxi_zhifeng_events.5.b
	trigger = { SHX = { NOT = { has_war_with = QIE } } } #In case war starts midway through

	immediate = {
		set_variable = {
			var = SHX_QIE_negotiation_value
			value = 1 #Set it at one to start, which is the bare minimum on the scale
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.8 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.8.a"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.8.a #Demand East Shanxi

		#Always Available

		ai_chance = {
			base = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				FNG = {
					exists = no
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				613 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = QIE }
			}
		}

		add_war_support = -0.05
		SHX_QIE_negotiation_demand_plus_1_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.8 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.8.b"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.8.b #Demand Guanzhong/Xian
		trigger = {
			has_war_support > 0.59 #Need 60% WS or Higher
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				QIE = {
					has_war_with_major = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				SHX = {
					has_war_support > 0.69
				}
			}
		}

		add_war_support = -0.10
		SHX_QIE_negotiation_demand_plus_2_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.8 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.8.c"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.8.c #Demand Both
		trigger = {
			has_war_support > 0.64 #Need 65% WS or Higher
		}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				QIE = {
					has_war_with_major = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				SHX = {
					has_war_support > 0.74
				}
			}
		}

		add_war_support = -0.15
		SHX_QIE_negotiation_demand_plus_3_effect = yes
	}
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			QIE = { country_event = { id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.9 days = 3 } }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.9 #Taiyuan-Beijing Talks: Round 2 (QIE)
	title = shanxi_zhifeng_events.9.t
	desc = shanxi_zhifeng_events.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_QIE_hu_shih_speech
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by event shanxi_zhifeng_events.8
	trigger = { SHX = { NOT = { has_war_with = QIE } } } #In case war starts midway through

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.9 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.9.a"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.9.a #Accept As is
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			#Baseline Values for Talks
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 4 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 2
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 5 }
			}

			#SHX-QIE Relations
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = QIE_purge_zhili } } #QIE is more willing to accept terms if they have purged the Zhili, seen as weaker
			}

			#How useful would an alliance with SHX be?
			modifier = { #How many QIE troops are being wasted guarding SHX's border?
				factor = 1.25
				num_divisions_in_states = {
					count > 9
					states = { 615 1060 607 799 } #Datong, Hebi, Luoyang, Guanzhong
				}
			}
			modifier = { #How many QIE troops are being wasted guarding SHX's border?
				factor = 1.25
				num_divisions_in_states = {
					count > 14
					states = { 615 1060 607 799 } #Datong, Hebi, Luoyang, Guanzhong
				}
			}
			modifier = { #How many soldiers does SHX have in the army?
				factor = 1.25
				SHX = { has_army_manpower = { size > 200000 } } #For Reference, SHX' starting max manpower is 194k
			}
			modifier = { #How many divisions does SHX have in the army?
				factor = 1.25
				SHX = { num_divisions > 19 } #For reference, SHX's starting division cap is 15
			}
			modifier = { #How many military factories does SHX have?
				factor = 1.25
				SHX = { num_of_military_factories > 9 } #For reference, SHX's mic is 3
			}
			modifier = { #Does QIE even hold East Shanxi? If not, may as well give it SHX so we don't lose the war
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { NOT = { controls_state = 615 } }
			}
			modifier = { #Does QIE even hold Guanzhong (Xi'an)? If not, may as well give it SHX so we don't lose the war
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { NOT = { controls_state = 799 } }
			}
		}

		SHX_QIE_negotiation_accept_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.9 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.9.b"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.9.b #Counteroffer
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable < 40 }
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 24 } #QIE needs at least 25% influence
			check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value > 1 } #Current Offer on the Table is 2 or more
		}
		SHX = { SHX_QIE_spend_large = yes } #QIE spends 15% Influence
		SHX_QIE_negotiation_demand_minus_1_effect = yes #Pushes the deal down 1 level
		hidden_effect = {
			SHX = {
				country_event = { id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.10 days = 3 } #Taiyuan-Beijing Talks: Round 3
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.9 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.9.c"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.9.c #Drive a Hard Bargain
		ai_chance = { base = 40 }
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 39 } #QIE needs at least 40% influence
			check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value > 2 } #Current Offer on the Table is 3 or more
		}
		SHX = { SHX_QIE_spend_giga = yes } #QIE spends 30% Influence
		SHX_QIE_negotiation_demand_minus_2_effect = yes #Pushes the deal down 2 level
		hidden_effect = {
			SHX = {
				country_event = { id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.10 days = 3 } #Taiyuan-Beijing Talks: Round 3
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.9 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.9.e"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.9.e #Walk out of talks
		trigger = {
			NOT = { SHX = { is_subject_of = QIE } } #In case SHX gets puppeted midway through
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			#Baseline Values for Talks
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 4 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 18
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 5 }
			}

			#QIE Influence
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 49 } #Sunk Cost
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 64 } #Sunk Cost
			}

			#QIE Diplomatic Status
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { has_war = yes } #QIE less likely to say no if they are at war
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { any_enemy_country = { owns_state = 613 } } #QIE less likely to say no if they are fighting a tag that owns Nanjing (probably a LEP unifier)
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { any_allied_country = { owns_state = 613 } } #QIE more likely to say no if they are fighting a tag that owns Nanjing (probably a LEP unifier)
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				FNG = { exists = no } #QIE more likely to say no if Fengtian is dead
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { has_war_with = FNG } #QIE more less to say no at war with FNG
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				JAP = { has_war_with_major = yes } #QIE more likely to say no if Japan is distracted
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { has_war_with = JAP } #QIE less likely to say no if at war with JAP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { alliance_strength_ratio > 1.25 } #QIE more likely to say no if stronger than foes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { alliance_strength_ratio > 1.5 } #QIE more likely to say no if way stronger than foes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { controls_state = 716 } #QIE more likely to say no if controls Shenyang
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { controls_state = 608 } #QIE more likely to say no if controls Beijing
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { controls_state = 1048 } #QIE more likely to say no if controls Wuhan
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { controls_state = 613 } #QIE more likely to say no if controls Nanjing
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { controls_state = 592 } #QIE more likely to say no if controls Canton/Guangzhou
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { surrender_progress > 0.25 } #QIE less likely to say no if losing ground
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { surrender_progress > 0.50 } #QIE less likely to say no if losing ground
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = SHX_FORPOL_QIE }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			SHX = {
				country_event = { id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.14 days = 3 } #Negotiations Collapse (QIE's Fault)
			}
			QIE = {
				country_event = { id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.14 days = 3 } #Negotiations Collapse (QIE's Fault)
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.10 #Taiyuan-Beijing Talks: Round 3 (SHX)
	title = shanxi_zhifeng_events.10.t
	desc = shanxi_zhifeng_events.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_wang_xiang
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by event shanxi_zhifeng_events.9
	trigger = { SHX = { NOT = { has_war_with = QIE } } } #In case war starts midway through

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.10 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.10.a"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.10.a #Accept As is
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			#Baseline Values for Talks
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 1 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 15
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 18
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 20
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 4 }
			}

			#SHX-QIE Relations
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = QIE_purge_zhili } } #SHX is more willing to accept terms if Zhili clique remains in power, seen as stronger
			}

			#Can QIE beat SHX in a fight?
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				has_war_support < 0.59 #SHX more likely to accept if their war support is lower
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				ic_ratio = {
					tag = QIE
					ratio < 0.20 #SHX more likley to accept if QIE's factory ratio is way higher. For reference, SHX starts with 5 and QIE starts with 22 (ratio 0.22)
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { num_subjects > 2 } #SHX more likely to accept if QIE has secure the recognition of a significant number of governments (ANQ/LEP, SHD, SZC, YUN, GXC, XSM all possible)
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = QIE
					ratio > 2 #SHX starts with a cap of 15 divisions, QIE starts with a cap of 57 and has 3 fronts to fight. SHX more likely to say yes if QIE has a decent sized force
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = QIE
					ratio > 3 #SHX starts with a cap of 15 divisions, QIE starts with a cap of 57 and has 3 fronts to fight. SHX more likely to say yes if QIE dwarfs them
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { enemies_strength_ratio < 0.75 } #SHX more likely to say yes if QIE outnumbers the enemy by a decent amount, making SHX less likely to win a potential wawr
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { enemies_strength_ratio < 0.50 } #SHX more likely to say yes if QIE outnumbers the enemy by a decent amount, making SHX less likely to win a potential wawr
			}
		}
		SHX_QIE_negotiation_accept_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.10 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.10.b"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.10.b #Counteroffer
		ai_chance = {
			base = 40
			modifier = {
				add = 40
				has_war_support < 0.55
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_war_support > 0.54 #SHX needs at least 55% influence
			check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value < 5 } #Current Offer on the Table is 4 or less
		}
		add_war_support = -0.05 #SHX Loses 5% war support
		SHX_QIE_negotiation_demand_plus_1_effect = yes #Pushes the deal up 1 level
		hidden_effect = {
			QIE = {
				country_event = { id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.11 days = 3 } #Taiyuan-Beijing Talks: Round 4
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.10 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.10.c"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.10.c #Drive a Hard Bargain
		ai_chance = { base = 40 }
		trigger = {
			has_war_support > 0.59 #QIE needs at least 59% influence
			check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value < 5 } #Current Offer on the Table is 3 or less
		}
		add_war_support = -0.10 #SHX Loses 10% war support
		SHX_QIE_negotiation_demand_plus_2_effect = yes #Pushes the deal up 2 level
		hidden_effect = {
			QIE = {
				country_event = { id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.11 days = 3 } #Taiyuan-Beijing Talks: Round 4
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.10 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.10.e"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.10.e #Walk out of talks
		trigger = {
			NOT = { SHX = { is_subject_of = QIE } } #In case SHX gets puppeted midway through
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			#Baseline Values for Talks
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 1 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 2
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 0
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 4 }
			}

			#QIE Influence
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 49 } #Sunk Cost
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 64 } #Sunk Cost
			}

			#QIE diplomatic status
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { has_war = yes } #SHX is more likely to say no if QIE is at war
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { any_enemy_country = { owns_state = 613 } } #SHX more likely to say no if QIE is fighting a tag that owns Nanjing (probably a LEP unifier)
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { any_allied_country = { owns_state = 613 } } #SHX less likely to say no if QIE is allied with a tag that owns Nanjing (probably a LEP unifier)
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				FNG = { exists = yes } #SHX more likely to say no if Fengtian is alive
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { has_war_with = FNG } #SHX more less to say no if QIE is at war with FNG
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { has_war_with = JAP } #SHX more likely to say no if SHX is at war with JAP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { alliance_strength_ratio < 0.80 } #SHX more likely to say no if QIE is weaker than foes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { alliance_strength_ratio < 0.66 } #SHX more likely to say no if QIE is weaker than foes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { controls_state = 716 } #SHX less likely to say no if QIE controls Shenyang
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { controls_state = 608 } #SHX less likely to say no if QIE controls Beijing
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { controls_state = 1048 } #SHX less likely to say no if QIE controls Wuhan
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { controls_state = 613 } #SHX less likely to say no if QIE controls Nanjing
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { controls_state = 592 } #SHX less likely to say no if QIE controls Canton/Guangzhou
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { surrender_progress > 0.25 } #SHX more likely to say no if QIE is losing ground
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { surrender_progress > 0.50 } #SHX more likely to say no if QIE is losing ground
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = SHX_FORPOL_QIE }
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			QIE = {
				country_event = { id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.13 days = 3 } #Negotiations Collapse (SHX's Fault)
			}
			SHX = {
				country_event = { id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.13 days = 3 } #Negotiations Collapse (SHX's Fault)
			}
		}

				QIE = { any_allied_country = { owns_state = 613 } } #QIE more likely to say no if they are fighting a tag that owns Nanjing (probably a LEP unifier)
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				FNG = { exists = no } #QIE more likely to say no if Fengtian is dead
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { has_war_with = FNG } #QIE more less to say no at war with FNG
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				JAP = { has_war_with_major = yes } #QIE more likely to say no if Japan is distracted
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { has_war_with = JAP } #QIE less likely to say no if at war with JAP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { alliance_strength_ratio > 1.25 } #QIE more likely to say no if stronger than foes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { alliance_strength_ratio > 1.5 } #QIE more likely to say no if way stronger than foes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { controls_state = 716 } #QIE more likely to say no if controls Shenyang
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { controls_state = 608 } #QIE more likely to say no if controls Beijing
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { controls_state = 1048 } #QIE more likely to say no if controls Wuhan
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { controls_state = 613 } #QIE more likely to say no if controls Nanjing
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { controls_state = 592 } #QIE more likely to say no if controls Canton/Guangzhou
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { surrender_progress > 0.25 } #QIE less likely to say no if losing ground
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { surrender_progress > 0.50 } #QIE less likely to say no if losing ground
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = SHX_FORPOL_QIE }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			SHX = {
				country_event = { id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.14 days = 3 } #Negotiations Collapse (QIE's Fault)
			}
			QIE = {
				country_event = { id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.14 days = 3 } #Negotiations Collapse (QIE's Fault)
			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.12 #Taiyuan-Beijing Talks: Round 5 (SHX)
	title = shanxi_zhifeng_events.12.t
	desc = shanxi_zhifeng_events.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_taiyuan_shouyi_gate
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by event shanxi_zhifeng_events.11
	trigger = { SHX = { NOT = { has_war_with = QIE } } } #In case war starts midway through

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.12 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.12.a"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.12.a #Accept As is
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			#Baseline Values for Talks
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 1 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 75
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 90
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 4 }
			}

			#SHX-QIE Relations
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = QIE_purge_zhili } } #SHX is more willing to accept terms if Zhili clique remains in power, seen as stronger
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.10
				always = yes #SHX is more willing to accept terms the longer negotiations go on as to avoid sunk costs. Requirements loosened below as well
			}

			#Can QIE beat SHX in a fight?
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				has_war_support < 0.51 #SHX more likely to accept if their war support is lower
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				ic_ratio = {
					tag = QIE
					ratio < 0.40 #SHX more likley to accept if QIE's factory ratio is way higher. For reference, SHX starts with 5 and QIE starts with 22 (ratio 0.22)
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { num_subjects > 1 }#SHX more likely to accept if QIE has secure the recognition of a significant number of governments (ANQ/LEP, SHD, SZC, YUN, GXC, XSM all possible)
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.3
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = QIE
					ratio > 2 #SHX starts with a cap of 15 divisions, QIE starts with a cap of 57 and has 3 fronts to fight. SHX more likely to say yes if QIE has a decent sized force
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.3
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = QIE
					ratio > 3 #SHX starts with a cap of 15 divisions, QIE starts with a cap of 57 and has 3 fronts to fight. SHX more likely to say yes if QIE dwarfs them
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { enemies_strength_ratio < 0.90 } #SHX more likely to say yes if QIE outnumbers the enemy by a decent amount, making SHX less likely to win a potential wawr
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { enemies_strength_ratio < 0.65 } #SHX more likely to say yes if QIE outnumbers the enemy by a decent amount, making SHX less likely to win a potential wawr
			}
		}
		SHX_QIE_negotiation_accept_effect = yes
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.12 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.12.b"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.12.b #Walk out of talks
		trigger = {
			NOT = { SHX = { is_subject_of = QIE } } #In case SHX gets puppeted midway through
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			#Baseline Values for Talks
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 1 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 2 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 0
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_negotiation_value = 4 }
			}

			#QIE Influence
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 49 } #Sunk Cost
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				check_variable = { SHX.SHX_QIE_influence_variable > 64 } #Sunk Cost
			}

			#QIE diplomatic status
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { has_war = yes } #SHX is more likely to say no if QIE is at war
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { any_enemy_country = { owns_state = 613 } } #SHX more likely to say no if QIE is fighting a tag that owns Nanjing (probably a LEP unifier)
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { any_allied_country = { owns_state = 613 } } #SHX less likely to say no if QIE is allied with a tag that owns Nanjing (probably a LEP unifier)
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				FNG = { exists = yes } #SHX more likely to say no if Fengtian is alive
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { has_war_with = FNG } #SHX more less to say no if QIE is at war with FNG
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { has_war_with = JAP } #SHX more likely to say no if SHX is at war with JAP
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { alliance_strength_ratio < 0.80 } #SHX more likely to say no if QIE is weaker than foes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { alliance_strength_ratio < 0.66 } #SHX more likely to say no if QIE is weaker than foes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { controls_state = 716 } #SHX less likely to say no if QIE controls Shenyang
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { controls_state = 608 } #SHX less likely to say no if QIE controls Beijing
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { controls_state = 1048 } #SHX less likely to say no if QIE controls Wuhan
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { controls_state = 613 } #SHX less likely to say no if QIE controls Nanjing
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.8
				QIE = { controls_state = 592 } #SHX less likely to say no if QIE controls Canton/Guangzhou
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { surrender_progress > 0.25 } #SHX more likely to say no if QIE is losing ground
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.25
				QIE = { surrender_progress > 0.50 } #SHX more likely to say no if QIE is losing ground
			}
			modifier = {

			}

		}

		complete_national_focus = SHX_destiny
	}
}

		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.26 #Beyond the Provincial Borders
	title = shanxi_zhifeng_events.26.t
	desc = shanxi_zhifeng_events.26.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_QIE_soldiers_planning

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = var:716.owner #Shenyang
			has_war_with = var:608.owner #Beijing
			has_war_with = var:1048.owner #Wuhan
			has_war_with = var:613.owner #Nanjing
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.26 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.26.a"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.26.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				608 = {
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = SHX
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				608 = { owner = { alliance_strength_ratio < 1.25 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.25
				608 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = FNG }
				FNG = { is_guaranteed_by = JAP }
				JAP = { NOT = { has_war_with_major = yes } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #check if they have unifier game rule
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = DEFAULT } }
				NOT = { has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = SHX_FORPOL_SHX } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { #If Beijing is not owned by SHX
				NOT = { has_wargoal_against = 608.owner }
				608 = { is_owned_by_ROOT_or_subject = no }
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = topple_government
				target = 608.owner
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { #Go for Wuhan if Beijing is owned already
				owns_state = 608
				NOT = { has_wargoal_against = 1048.owner }
				1048 = { is_owned_by_ROOT_or_subject = no }
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = topple_government
				target = 1048.owner
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { #Go for Nanjing if Beijing and Wuhan are owned already
				owns_state = 608
				owns_state = 1048
				NOT = { has_wargoal_against = 613.owner }
				613 = { is_owned_by_ROOT_or_subject = no }
			}
			create_wargoal = {
				type = topple_government
				target = 613.owner
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.26 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.26.b"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.26.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				has_war = yes
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				608 = { owner = { alliance_strength_ratio > 1.25 } }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0 #check if they have unifier game rule
				has_game_rule = { rule = SHX_forpol option = SHX_FORPOL_SHX }
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = SHX_war_of_liberation
		add_ideas = SHX_fortress_shanxi
	}
}

country_event = { #Confronting the Commercial Class
	id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.105
	title = shanxi_zhifeng_events.105.t
	desc = shanxi_zhifeng_events.105.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_wang_xiang
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes #Necessary to avoid bugs

	option = { #kill him kill him!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.105 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.105.a"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.105.a
		if = {
			limit = { SHX_wang_xiang = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			add_political_power = -100
			add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = -0.10 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { SHX_wang_xiang = { is_political_advisor = yes } }
			SHX_wang_xiang = { remove_political_advisor_role = yes }
			add_political_power = -50
			add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = -0.05 }
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -25
			add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = -0.03 }
		}
		SHX_wang_xiang = { remove_political_advisor_role = yes }
	}
	option = { # Sideline him for now but he may be of service in the future.
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.105 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.105.b"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.105.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				SHX_wang_xiang = { is_second_in_command = yes }
				SHX_wang_xiang = { is_political_advisor = yes }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { SHX_wang_xiang = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			deactivate_advisor = SHX_wang_xiang_sic
			add_political_power = -50
			add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = -0.5 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { SHX_wang_xiang = { is_political_advisor = yes } }
			deactivate_advisor = SHX_wang_xiang_advisor
			add_political_power = -25
			add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = -0.03 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_this_may_unlock_some_allies_in_the_future_tt
	}
	option = { #: He's too invaluable to lose, let us keep him close but under watch.
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.105 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.105.c"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.105.c
		if = {
			limit = { SHX_wang_xiang = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.10 }
			add_war_support = -0.1
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { SHX_wang_xiang = { is_political_advisor = yes } }
			add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.05 }
			add_war_support = -0.05
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.03 }
			add_war_support = -0.03 #Fallback
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_this_may_unlock_some_allies_in_the_future_tt
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = shanxi_zhifeng_events.106 #The War of Resistance
	title = shanxi_zhifeng_events.106.t
	desc = shanxi_zhifeng_events.106.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_QIE_zhili_soldiers
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered when the CUF is first formed.
	fire_only_once = yes #Would be awful if this kept spamming.

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_war_with = JAP #Wont' get this event if you decide not to join the CUF or at least be at war with the existential threat
			has_war_with_major = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.106 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.106.a"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.106.a #We marshal all forces to victory!
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = SHX_war_of_liberation }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SHX_war_of_liberation
				add_idea = SHX_war_of_resistance
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = SHX_war_of_resistance
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_zhifeng_events.106 option shanxi_zhifeng_events.106.b"
		name = shanxi_zhifeng_events.106.b #We have other concerns at play.
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		add_war_support = 0.20
	}
}
