				SHX = { is_ai = no } #Give the player something more fun to do usually.
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 25
				FNG = { exists = no }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				QIE = { owns_state = 613 } #Owning Nanjing is a good sign QIE is strong
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				XSM = { is_ai = no } #Give the Ma a chance
			}
		}
		create_wargoal = {
			type = puppet_wargoal_focus
			target = XSM
		}
		SHX = {
			country_event = { id = shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.11 days = 3 } #The Central Government marches on Suiyuan!
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				XSM = { is_subject_of = QIE }
			}
			set_autonomy = {
				target = XSM
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				end_wars = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				XSM = { is_in_faction_with = QIE }
			}
			remove_from_faction = XSM
		}
	}
	option = { #Call Taiyuan. Let Governor Yan hold up his end of the bargain
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.10 option shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.10.b"
		name = shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.10.b
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_QIE_neutrality_warning_tooltip
		SHX = {
			country_event = { id = shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.12 days = 3 } #We are on our own
			set_country_flag = SHX_suiyuan_QIE_defied_by_ma
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				XSM = { is_subject_of = QIE }
			}
			set_autonomy = {
				target = XSM
				autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				end_wars = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				XSM = { is_in_faction_with = QIE }
			}
			remove_from_faction = XSM
		}
	}
}

		}

				owns_state = 283 #Lanzhou

			}
		}

				}

				}
				add_state_claim = 612 #SHX gets Xilingol as well if they are demanding it from a victorious XSM to avoid bordergore

				MON = {
					owns_state = 616 #Ordos
				}
			}
			TIB = {
				country_event = { id = shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.33 days = 3 } #Shanxi warns us off
			}
		}
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = 616 decision = SHX_suiyuan_destabilise_province }
		if = {
			limit = { MON = { owns_state = 348 } }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 348 decision = SHX_suiyuan_destabilise_province }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { TIB = { owns_state = 604 } }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = 604 decision = SHX_suiyuan_destabilise_province }
		}

			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = XSM }
			set_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_XSM
			SHX = { country_event = shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.51 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = MON }
			set_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_MON
			if = {
				limit = { is_guaranteed_by = TIB }
				TIB = {
					country_event = { id = shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.50 days = 2 }
				}
			}
			else = { SHX = { country_event = shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.51 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = TIB }
			set_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_TIB
			SHX = { country_event = shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.51 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.50 option shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.50.b"
		name = shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.50.b #Perhaps it is time to end this
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		add_war_support = -0.10
		if = {
			limit = { tag = SHX }
			616 = {
				owner = {
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { tag = SHX } }
						country_event = { id = shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.50 days = 2 }
					}
					else_if = {
						limit = { has_war_with = TIB }
						TIB = { country_event = { id = shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.50 days = 2 } }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = XSM }
			SHX = { country_event = shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.51 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = MON }
			if = {
				limit = { is_guaranteed_by = TIB }
				TIB = { country_event = { id = shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.50 days = 2 } }
			}
			else = { SHX = { country_event = shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.51 } }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = TIB }
			SHX = { country_event = shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.51 }
		}
		add_stability = 0.10
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_out_effects_tooltip
	}
}

			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_yan_coat
	is_triggered_only = yes #Event shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.50

	major = yes
	show_major = {

			owns_state = 616 #Ordos
			AND = {
				has_guaranteed = MON
				MON = {
					owns_state = 616
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.51 option shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.51.a"
		name = shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.51.a #Peace prevails then.
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_SHX
				has_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_XSM
				has_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_MON
				has_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_TIB
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = SHX }
			MON = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = SHX
						is_controlled_by = SHX
					}
					transfer_state_to = SHX
				}
			}
			XSM = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = SHX
						is_controlled_by = SHX
					}
					transfer_state_to = SHX
				}
			}
			TIB = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = SHX
						is_controlled_by = SHX
					}
					transfer_state_to = SHX
				}
			}
			every_enemy_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						owns_state = 616 #Ordos
						is_ally_with = TIB
						is_ally_with = MON
						is_ally_with = XSM
						has_guaranteed = XSM
						has_guaranteed = MON
						has_guaranteed = TIB
					}
				}
				white_peace = SHX #If SHX has any puppet states I might actually die.
			}
			clear_variable = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_prep_variable
			SHX_suiyuan_campaign_tally_success_effect = yes
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.53 days = 5 } }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.51 option shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.51.b"
		name = shanxi_suiyuan_campaign_events.51.b #What's another year of war?
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_SHX
				has_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_XSM
				has_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_MON
				has_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_TIB
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = SHX }
			activate_mission = SHX_suiyuan_northwestern_war_exhaustion_mission
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SHX_suiyuan_northwestern_war_exhaustion_mission
				days = SHX.SHX_suiyuan_campaign_prep_variable
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				616 = {
					owner = {
						activate_mission = SHX_suiyuan_northwestern_war_exhaustion_mission
						add_days_mission_timeout = {
							mission = SHX_suiyuan_northwestern_war_exhaustion_mission
							days = SHX.SHX_suiyuan_campaign_prep_variable
						}
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_guaranteed_by = TIB
							}
							TIB = {
								activate_mission = SHX_suiyuan_northwestern_war_exhaustion_mission
								add_days_mission_timeout = {
									mission = SHX_suiyuan_northwestern_war_exhaustion_mission
									days = SHX.SHX_suiyuan_campaign_prep_variable
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		clr_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_SHX
		clr_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_XSM
		clr_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_MON
		clr_global_flag = SHX_suiyuan_campaign_peace_rejected_TIB
	}

			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = shanxi_endgame_events.7 #The National Convention Opens
	title = shanxi_endgame_events.7.t
	desc = shanxi_endgame_events.7.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_CHN_China_five_colour_flags
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_leader = { character = SHX_feng_yuxiang } }
				#Feng is more likely to go party-state
				random_list = {
					#45% Goes Party-State
					15 = { set_country_flag = SHX_ai_chooses_YCP_ending_flag }
					30 = { set_country_flag = SHX_ai_chooses_KMT_ending_flag }
					#55% Goes New Beiyang
					35 = { set_country_flag = SHX_ai_chooses_DCP_ending_flag }
					5 = { set_country_flag = SHX_ai_chooses_RP_ending_flag }
					15 = { set_country_flag = SHX_ai_chooses_Hu_ending_flag }
				}
				random_list = {
					35 = { set_country_flag = SHX_ai_chooses_southern_ending_flag }
					65 = { set_country_flag = SHX_ai_chooses_northern_ending_flag }
				}
			}
			else = {
				#Yan is more likely to go hard-line on Southerners
				random_list = {
					#35% Goes Party-State
					25 = { set_country_flag = SHX_ai_chooses_YCP_ending_flag }
					10 = { set_country_flag = SHX_ai_chooses_KMT_ending_flag }
					#65% Goes New Beiyang
					35 = { set_country_flag = SHX_ai_chooses_DCP_ending_flag }
					20 = { set_country_flag = SHX_ai_chooses_RP_ending_flag }
					10 = { set_country_flag = SHX_ai_chooses_Hu_ending_flag }
				}
				random_list = {
					25 = { set_country_flag = SHX_ai_chooses_southern_ending_flag }
					75 = { set_country_flag = SHX_ai_chooses_northern_ending_flag }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_endgame_events.7 option shanxi_endgame_events.7.a"
		name = shanxi_endgame_events.7.a
		hidden_effect = { #Let the Conference begin
			country_event = { id = shanxi_endgame_events.8 days = 3 } #The Northern Parties Rally
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = shanxi_endgame_events.8 #A New Beiyang
	title = shanxi_endgame_events.8.t
	desc = shanxi_endgame_events.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_QIE_beiyang_assembly
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = shanxi_endgame_events.9 days = 7 } #The Southern Republicans Rally
			QIE = {
				QIE_wu_xianzi = { set_nationality = ROOT }
				QIE_hu_shih = { set_nationality = ROOT }
				QIE_wellington_koo = { set_nationality = ROOT }
			}
			FNG = { FNG_zhang_zongxiang = { set_nationality = ROOT } }
			QIE_hu_shih = { promote_character = { ideology = social_liberal_subtype } }
			FNG_zhang_zongxiang = { promote_character = { ideology = market_liberal_subtype } }
			QIE_wu_xianzi = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						desc = QIE_wu_xianzi_leader_desc
						ideology = social_conservative_subtype
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				long_name = SHX_independent_republicans_party_long
				name = SHX_independent_republicans_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				long_name = SHX_recovery_party_long
				name = SHX_recovery_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				long_name = SHX_democratic_constitutionalist_party_long
				name = SHX_democratic_constitutionalist_party
			}
		}
	}

	option = {

			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.03
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_endgame_events.8 option shanxi_endgame_events.8.b"
		name = shanxi_endgame_events.8.b #An alliance with the pragmatic Liang Shiyi will be easy to control.
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_country_flag = SHX_ai_chooses_RP_ending_flag
			}
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.01
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_endgame_events.8 option shanxi_endgame_events.8.c"
		name = shanxi_endgame_events.8.c #We will maintain amicable relationships with the idealistic Hu Shih.

country_event = { #A National Vice
	id = shanxi_endgame_events.16
	title = shanxi_endgame_events.16.t
	desc = {
		text = shanxi_endgame_events.16.d.yan
		trigger = { has_country_flag = SHX_yan_victory_over_gmj }
	}
	desc = {
		text = shanxi_endgame_events.16.d.feng
		trigger = { has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_opium_den

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {  #Attempt to Regulate Sales
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_endgame_events.16 option shanxi_endgame_events.16.a"
		name = shanxi_endgame_events.16.a
		add_offsite_building = { type = industrial_complex level = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = -0.05
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = -0.05
			}
		}
	}
	option = {  #A Medicinal Approach is Best
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_endgame_events.16 option shanxi_endgame_events.16.b"
		name = shanxi_endgame_events.16.b
		add_stability = 0.10
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
	}

	option = {  #A Harsh Approach is Best
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_endgame_events.16 option shanxi_endgame_events.16.c"
		name = shanxi_endgame_events.16.c
		add_war_support = 0.10
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = SHX_feng_victory_over_yan }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = national_populist
				popularity = 0.03
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #The National Army and the Nationalist Party
	id = shanxi_endgame_events.25
	title = shanxi_endgame_events.25.t
	desc = shanxi_endgame_events.25.d
	is_triggered_only = yes #Triggered by Focus: SHX_kindle_the_mass_movement_focus
	picture = GFX_report_event_SHX_feng_kmt

	trigger = {
		is_subject = no #Make sure you are not a puppet so no ideology flip
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_endgame_events.25 option shanxi_endgame_events.25.a"
		name = shanxi_endgame_events.25.a  #Join the KMT
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		add_stability = -0.10
		add_political_power = -100
		promote_character = {
			character = SHX_feng_yuxiang
			ideology = radical_socialist_subtype
		}
		SHX_feng_yuxiang = { china_set_character_alignment_left_kuomintang = yes }
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = radical_socialist
			elections_allowed = no
			name = SHX_kuomintang_feng
			long_name = SHX_kuomintang_feng_long
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = SHX_kuomintang_feng_long
				name = SHX_kuomintang_feng
			}
		}

		#Converts 75% of Auth Dem Popularity into Rad SOc
		set_temp_variable = { SHX_auth_dem_popularity_temp_var = party_popularity@authoritarian_democrat }
		multiply_temp_variable = { SHX_auth_dem_popularity_temp_var = 0.75 }
		set_temp_variable = { SHX_neg_auth_dem_popularity_temp_var = SHX_auth_dem_popularity_temp_var }
		multiply_temp_variable = { SHX_neg_auth_dem_popularity_temp_var = -1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = SHX_neg_auth_dem_popularity_temp_var }
		add_popularity = { ideology = radical_socialist popularity = SHX_auth_dem_popularity_temp_var }

		#Adds Auth Dems into Faction
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes

		#Sets Cosmetic tag to KMT
		set_cosmetic_tag = LKT_united_china
		custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_this_may_unlock_some_allies_in_the_future_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = shanxi_endgame_events.26 days = 400 } #Deng Xiaoping Event
			every_subject_country = {
				limit = {
					has_socialist_government = no
					NOT = {
						original_tag = JAP
						original_tag = KOR
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = radical_socialist
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_subject = JAP }
				JAP = { JAP_socialist_government = yes }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_subject = KOR }
				KOR = {
					drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
					KOR_socialist_government = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_subject = INC }
				INC = {
					INC_puppet_setup = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_endgame_events.25 option shanxi_endgame_events.25.b"
		name = shanxi_endgame_events.25.b  #Keep the movements separate.
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.05 }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = shanxi_endgame_events.100 #Reform the Central Army
	title = shanxi_endgame_events.100.t
	desc = shanxi_endgame_events.100.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_QIE_zhili_soldiers
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_endgame_events.100 option shanxi_endgame_events.100.a"
		name = shanxi_endgame_events.100.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_idea = SHX_integrated_army
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = SHX_dual_armies2 }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SHX_dual_armies2
				add_idea = SHX_regional_army_idea
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = SHX_integrated_army }
			add_command_power = -100
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SHX_integrated_army
				add_idea = SHX_regional_army_idea
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = CHN_an_army_in_transition_idea
				days = 365
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_harder_to_switch_tracks_tt
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_endgame_events.100 option shanxi_endgame_events.100.b"
		name = shanxi_endgame_events.100.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_idea = SHX_dual_armies2
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = SHX_integrated_army }
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SHX_integrated_army
				add_idea = SHX_new_central_army
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_idea = SHX_dual_armies2 }
			add_command_power = -100
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SHX_dual_armies2
				add_idea = SHX_new_central_army
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = CHN_an_army_in_transition_idea
				days = 365
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = SHX_harder_to_switch_tracks_tt
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = shanxi_endgame_events.101  #Amnesty for Pioneering Generals
	title = shanxi_endgame_events.101.t
	desc = shanxi_endgame_events.101.d

	fire_only_once = yes #Prevents Spam
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_QIE_warlord_soldiers

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event shanxi_endgame_events.101 option shanxi_endgame_events.101.a"
		name = shanxi_endgame_events.101.a #A new generation of commanders for the New China.
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { country_exists = QIE }
				NOT = {
					SZC = {
						SZC_zhili_in_exile = yes
						exists = yes
					}
				}
			}
			QIE = {
				set_temp_variable = { qin_dechun = QIE_qin_dechun }
				set_temp_variable = { du_xijun = QIE_du_xijun }
				set_temp_variable = { guo_jijiao = QIE_guo_jijiao }
				set_temp_variable = { li_shuchun = QIE_li_shuchun }
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				add_corps_commander_role = { character = var:qin_dechun }
				add_corps_commander_role = { character = var:du_xijun }
				add_corps_commander_role = { character = var:guo_jijiao }
				add_corps_commander_role = { character = var:li_shuchun }
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { SZC = { has_character = QIE_du_xijun } }
					SZC = {
						QIE_qin_dechun = { set_nationality = SHX }
						QIE_du_xijun = { set_nationality = SHX }
						QIE_guo_jijiao = { set_nationality = SHX }
						QIE_li_shuchun = { set_nationality = SHX }
					}
				}
				else = {
					QIE = {
						QIE_qin_dechun = { set_nationality = SHX }
						QIE_du_xijun = { set_nationality = SHX }
						QIE_guo_jijiao = { set_nationality = SHX }
						QIE_li_shuchun = { set_nationality = SHX }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
